	model = GR-300
	nmea = 3.0
	notes = Also includes an (untested) bluetooth interface. Has two LEDs: blue for bluetooth, green for status. Solid green = on and searching for satellite fixes. Blinking green = on and has 3D fix.
Also a similar GR-310 version available, though don't have it. Possible that only GR-310 supports bluetooth.
Programs only seem to be able to communicate with the dongle at 4800 baud rates, though this is autodetected by gpsd with no problems.
Purchased from eBay, though Navisys is in Taiwan. Approx £40 per dongle.
http://www.navisys.com.tw/products/gps_usb_dongle.htm
	packaging = GPS mouse
	rating = excellent
	sample_notes = Device was not moving for this sample. Fixes switch between 2D and 3D and no fix (I'm inside in a variable satellite signal area).
